However, the user says it hangs. Let's look at the code.
In `rb4_songlist_generator.py`:
`run_cmd` is used for `PkgTool.Core pkg_extractinnerpfs` and `PkgTool.Core pfs_extract`.
It has a `timeout` parameter.
In `extract_songdta_from_pkg`:
- `pkg_extractinnerpfs` has `timeout=600`.
- `pfs_extract` has `timeout=600`.

If the process hangs without triggering the timeout or if the timeout is too high/not working as expected, it might look like a hang.
Also, the `run_cmd` with `show_output=True` uses a thread to stream output.

If the script is hanging, it might be due to:
1. A specific PKG that takes too long to extract.
2. A deadlock in the threading/streaming of output.
3. A resource issue (disk space, memory).
4. `PkgTool.Core` itself hanging.

The user mentioned that the "old script" worked. I don't have the old script, but I have the current one.

The user says "every time we try to run against the 98 pkg files now, it stops around pkg #28 or 29 and just hangs".
Looking at the list of PKGs:
`UP8802-CUSA02084_00-CREQ2604P03AVRIL.pkg` is #29 in one run. It's quite large (415MB).

Let's check the `run_cmd` implementation again.
```python
122: def run_cmd(cmd, check=True, capture=True, show_output=False, indent="\t\t", timeout=None):
...
128:         process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, shell=True, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=True, bufsize=1)
...
139:             process.wait(timeout=timeout)
140:         except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
141:             process.kill()
142:             raise RuntimeError(f"Command timed out after {timeout} seconds: {cmd}")
```
If `timeout` is `None`, `process.wait()` will wait forever.
In `extract_songdta_from_pkg`:
`run_cmd(f'DOTNET_SYSTEM_GLOBALIZATION_INVARIANT=1 PkgTool.Core pkg_extractinnerpfs "{pkg_path}" {pfs_file}', show_output=True, indent="\t\t", timeout=600)`
`run_cmd(f'DOTNET_SYSTEM_GLOBALIZATION_INVARIANT=1 PkgTool.Core pfs_extract {pfs_file} {pfs_extract_dir}', show_output=True, indent="\t\t\t", timeout=600)`

Both have 600s timeouts.

Maybe the hang is in `extract_binary_dta.py`?
`run_cmd(f'cd /workspace && python3 RB4/scripts/extract_binary_dta.py {files_arg} {temp_output}', show_output=True, indent="\t\t")`
Here, `timeout` is NOT provided, so it defaults to `None`.
If `extract_binary_dta.py` hangs, the whole script hangs.

Wait, `extract_binary_dta.py` uses `multiprocessing` or similar? No, it seems to be sequential in `main`.
But it's called from `rb4_songlist_generator.py`.

Let's look at `extract_binary_dta.py`. It reads files.
If it encounters a very large or weird file, could it hang?
It uses `f.read()` which reads the whole file into memory.

Actually, the user says it's a regression.

`get_pkg_file` uses `subprocess.run(cmd, shell=True).returncode == 0`. No timeout here.

No timeout.

```
40: echo "  Found $TOTAL .pkg file(s) to process"
41: 
42: for PKG_FILE in "${PKG_FILES[@]}"; do
43:     INDEX=$((INDEX + 1))
44:     PKG_BASENAME=$(basename "$PKG_FILE")
45:     
46:     echo "  [$INDEX/$TOTAL] Processing: $PKG_BASENAME"
47:     
48:     EXTRACT_DIR="$TMP_DIR/extracted_$INDEX"
49:     mkdir -p "$EXTRACT_DIR"
50:     
51:     # Run PkgTool to extract (zero passcode works for standard fPKGs)
52:     # Using pkg_makegp4 instead of pkg_extract to ensure multi-partition/songs folders are unpacked
53:     if "$PKG_TOOL" pkg_makegp4 --passcode 00000000000000000000000000000000 "$PKG_FILE" "$EXTRACT_DIR" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
54:         
55:         # Extract the Source Title from PARAM.SFO (if available)
56:         # NOTE: This is ONLY used as fallback when binary doesn't contain source metadata
57:         SFO_FILE=$(find "$EXTRACT_DIR" -name "param.sfo" | head -n 1)
58:         PKG_SOURCE=""  # Empty means "auto-detect from binary"
59:         if [ -n "$SFO_FILE" ]; then
60:             SFO_TITLE=$("$PKG_TOOL" sfo_listentries "$SFO_FILE" | grep "TITLE :" | cut -d ':' -f 2- | sed 's/^ *//')
61:             if [ -n "$SFO_TITLE" ]; then
62:                 # Store SFO title for reference, but don't override binary source
63:                 PKG_SOURCE="$SFO_TITLE"
64:             fi
65:         fi
66: 
67:         # Find if any song DTAs exist before running Python
68:         if find "$EXTRACT_DIR" -name "*.songdta_ps4" | grep -q .; then
69:             # Run the Python scraper - WITHOUT --source override so binary source is used
70:             SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
71:             PYTHON_OUT="$TMP_DIR/songs_$(printf '%06d' $INDEX).json"
72:             
73:             # Only pass --source if explicitly provided (empty string means auto)
74:             if [ -n "$PKG_SOURCE" ]; then
75:                 python3 "$SCRIPT_DIR/extract_binary_dta.py" "$EXTRACT_DIR" "$PYTHON_OUT" --source "$PKG_SOURCE"
76:             else
77:                 python3 "$SCRIPT_DIR/extract_binary_dta.py" "$EXTRACT_DIR" "$PYTHON_OUT"
78:             fi
79:             
80:             if [ -f "$PYTHON_OUT" ]; then
81:                 COUNT=$(jq 'length' "$PYTHON_OUT")
82:                 SONG_COUNT=$((SONG_COUNT + COUNT))
83:                 echo "  ✓ Extracted $COUNT song(s) [Source: $PKG_SOURCE]"
84:             fi
85:         else
86:             echo "  ⚠ No .songdta_ps4 files found in $PKG_BASENAME"
87:         fi
88:     else
89:         echo "  ⚠ Failed to unpack: $PKG_BASENAME"
90:     fi
91:     
92:     # CRITICAL: Delete extraction dir immediately to save disk space
93:     rm -rf "$EXTRACT_DIR"
94: done
95: 
96: # Combine all partial JSON files into the final output
97: if ls "$TMP_DIR"/songs_*.json >/dev/null 2>&1; then
98:     jq -s 'add' "$TMP_DIR"/songs_*.json > "$OUT_FILE"
99: else
100:     echo "[]" > "$OUT_FILE"
101: fi
102: 
103: echo "═══════════════════════════════════════════════"
104: echo " Scan complete"
105: echo "   Songs found   : $SONG_COUNT"
106: echo "   Output        : $OUT_FILE"
107: echo "═══════════════════════════════════════════════"

(End of file - total 107 lines)
```

## Assistant (Build · gemma-4-31b-it · 37.6s)

_Thinking:_

The user reports that the script hangs again, and the console output stops abruptly.
Looking at the previous tool call output (which I can't see in the prompt but the user describes), it seems the process is still running but not producing output, or it's truly stuck.
The user mentions "the output stops at a random character".

Possibilities:
1. The process is indeed hung (infinite loop or deadlocked).
2. The process is taking a very long time to extract a large PKG (some DLC PKGs can be several GBs).
3. There's a buffer issue with `subprocess.Popen` and `stdout.PIPE`.
4. The SMB connection is dropping or timing out.

Let's look at the `rb4_songlist_generator.py` implementation of `run_cmd`.
It uses `subprocess.Popen` with `stdout=subprocess.PIPE` and a separate thread to stream output.

```python
def run_cmd(cmd, check=True, capture=True, show_output=False, indent="\t\t", timeout=None):
    import subprocess
    import threading
    
    if show_output:
        process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, shell=True, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=True, bufsize=1)
        
        def stream_output(stream):
            for line in stream:
                print(f"{indent}{line.rstrip()}")
                sys.stdout.flush()
        
        thread = threading.Thread(target=stream_output, args=(process.stdout,))
        thread.start()
        
        try:
            process.wait(timeout=timeout)
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            process.kill()
            raise RuntimeError(f"Command timed out after {timeout} seconds: {cmd}")
            
        thread.join()
        
        if check and process.returncode != 0:
            raise RuntimeError(f"Command failed: {cmd}")
        return ""
    
    result = subprocess.run(cmd, shell=True, capture_output=capture, text=True, timeout=timeout)
    # ...
```

If `process.wait(timeout=timeout)` is called, it waits for the process to finish. If the process hangs and `timeout` is `None`, it waits forever.
In the last run, the user says it hangs around PKG #28 or #29.

Let's see which PKGs are being processed.
I'll add more logging to `rb4_songlist_generator.py` to print exactly which command is running and when it starts/ends.
Also, I'll check the `smb_pkg_finder.py` to see if it might be the cause.

The user says "the output stops at a random character". This often happens when a process crashes or is killed silently, or when there's a character encoding issue.

Actually, looking at the `run_cmd` implementation:
`process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, shell=True, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=True, bufsize=1)`
If the output contains characters that aren't valid UTF-8 (since `text=True` is used), it might crash the `stream_output` thread or the main process.

Let's try changing `text=True` to `text=False` and decoding manually with `errors='replace'`.

Also, I'll check the logs. The script logs to a file.
`LOG_FILE = os.path.join(args.temp_dir, f'rb4_extract_{ts}.log')`
I should check that log file to see where it stopped.


## Assistant (Build · gemma-4-31b-it · 30.8s)

_Thinking:_

The system load is low. No process is consuming 100% CPU.
I'll modify `run_cmd` in `rb4_songlist_generator.py` to handle potential encoding issues and add a more robust timeout mechanism.

Specifically:
1. Remove `text=True` from `Popen` and decode bytes manually.
2. Ensure the `stream_output` thread doesn't hang.
3. Add explicit logging for the start and end of each command.
4. Change `process.wait(timeout=timeout)` to a loop with `process.poll()` to allow better control or just keep the timeout.

Wait, if it hangs at PKG #28/29, maybe it's a specific file.
Let's see if we can find a way to detect the hang.
If I run the script and it hangs, I can use `ps` to see if the `PkgTool.Core` process is still alive.

Actually, the most likely cause of "stops at a random character" is a `UnicodeDecodeError` in the `stream_output` thread.
Because `text=True` is used, `Popen` automatically decodes the output. If it encounters a byte sequence that isn't valid UTF-8, it might raise an exception.
If that exception happens inside the `stream_output` thread, it will kill the thread silently (unless handled), and the main thread will just wait for `process.wait()`. If the process itself is still running and producing output that the thread is no longer reading, the pipe will fill up, and the process will block on `write()`. This is a classic deadlock.

I will fix this by:
1. Disabling `text=True` (using bytes).
2. Decoding bytes using `errors='replace'`.
3. Adding a small timeout to the line reading if possible, or just ensuring the thread doesn't die.

Let's apply these changes.

**Tool: edit**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "/workspace/RB4/scripts/rb4_songlist_generator.py",
  "oldString": "    if show_output:\n        process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, shell=True, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=True, bufsize=1)\n        \n        def stream_output(stream):\n            for line in stream:\n                print(f\"{indent}{line.rstrip()}\")\n                sys.stdout.flush()\n        \n        thread = threading.Thread(target=stream_output, args=(process.stdout,))\n        thread.start()\n        \n        try:\n            process.wait(timeout=timeout)\n        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:\n            process.kill()\n            raise RuntimeError(f\"Command timed out after {timeout} seconds: {cmd}\")\n            \n        thread.join()\n        \n        if check and process.returncode != 0:\n            raise RuntimeError(f\"Command failed: {cmd}\")\n        return \"\"",
  "newString": "    if show_output:\n        process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, shell=True, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=False, bufsize=1)\n        \n        def stream_output(stream):\n            try:\n                for line in stream:\n                    decoded_line = line.decode('utf-8', errors='replace').rstrip()\n                    print(f\"{indent}{decoded_line}\")\n                    sys.stdout.flush()\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"{indent}Error reading output: {e}\")\n        \n        thread = threading.Thread(target=stream_output, args=(process.stdout,))\n        thread.daemon = True\n        thread.start()\n        \n        try:\n            process.wait(timeout=timeout)\n        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:\n            process.kill()\n            raise RuntimeError(f\"Command timed out after {timeout} seconds: {cmd}\")\n            \n        thread.join(timeout=5)\n        \n        if check and process.returncode != 0:\n            raise RuntimeError(f\"Command failed: {cmd}\")\n        return \"\""
}
```

## Assistant (Build · gemma-4-31b-it · 52.9s)

_Thinking:_

The user is reporting that the `rb4_songlist_generator.py` script hangs or stops outputting to the console around the same point (roughly PKG #28 or #29) every time. They suspect a character limit or a lost console output, but they know the script *can* finish all 98 PKGs.

Looking at the previous tool outputs:
1.  The script processes PKGs one by one.
2.  It fetches a PKG from SMB, extracts an inner PFS, extracts the contents of that PFS, and then parses binary `.songdta_ps4` files.
3.  The "hang" happens during this process.
4.  I've already tried adding timeouts to the `run_cmd` and changing the `subprocess.Popen` output streaming to handle potential decoding issues.
5.  The user says it "stops at a random character". This strongly suggests a buffering or encoding issue with the console output in the environment, or a specific PKG that causes a hang/crash that isn't being reported correctly.

Let's analyze where it's hanging. If it always hangs around PKG #28, there might be a specific PKG that is causing the issue.

Wait, the user said "stops at a random character". This often happens in some terminal environments when a null byte or some non-printable character is sent to the stdout, which can confuse the terminal or the tool reporting the output.

However, if the process is actually *running* but just not *outputting*, we should be able to see it in `top` or `ps`.

In the last `top` output:
- `opencode` is running.
- There are several `node` processes.
- I don't see a `python3` process running *at the moment* of the `top` call (because the user probably interrupted it).

If it's hanging on a specific PKG, I can find out which one by looking at the `processed_pkgs.json` file (if incremental mode was on) or by running the script and seeing where it stops. But the user is running with `--no-incremental`.

Let's try a different approach:
1.  **Log everything to a file** and read the file periodically, rather than relying on the console output.
2.  **Simplify the output**. Instead of streaming every line of the `PkgTool` output, only log the start and end of each PKG.
3.  **Increase robustness** of the extraction process.

Wait, if it's a "random character" and it's "stopping", maybe it's a buffer overflow or a specific character sequence that's killing the output stream.

Let's check the log files. The script writes to a log file: `/workspace/rb4_temp/rb4_extract_<timestamp>.log`.
In the last run, the log file had only 2 lines:
```
1: Logging to: /workspace/rb4_temp/rb4_extract_20260408_094820.log
2: Started at 2026-04-08T09:48:20.227507
```
This means the `log(msg)` function is not being called.
Looking at `rb4_songlist_generator.py`:
```python
def log(msg):
    """Log to both console and file."""
    print(msg)
    if LOG_FILE:
        with open(LOG_FILE, 'a') as f:
            f.write(msg + '\n')
```
But `main()` uses `print()` for most of its progress updates, NOT `log()`. Only the start and the "Logging to..." message are using `log()`.

This is a problem. If the console output is lost, we have no way to know what's happening.

I will:
1.  Modify `rb4_songlist_generator.py` to use the `log()` function for *all* progress updates.
2.  Disable the `show_output=True` in `run_cmd` for the heavy extraction steps, or at least make it optional/less chatty, to avoid flooding the console with potential "bad" characters.
3.  Run the script again and monitor the log file.

Actually, let's look at the `run_cmd` implementation again.
```python
def run_cmd(cmd, check=True, capture=True, show_output=False, indent="\t\t", timeout=None):
    ...
    if show_output:
        process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, shell=True, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=True, bufsize=1)
        ...
```
The `show_output` part uses `subprocess.Popen`. If `text=True`, it decodes using the default encoding. If the `PkgTool` outputs binary garbage, it might crash the thread or the main process.

I already changed it to `text=False` and manually decode with `errors='replace'`.

Let's try to make the script more "silent" but log progress to a file.

Another possibility: the `smbclient` fetch is hanging?
```python
if args.smb:
    ...
    success = get_pkg_file(pkg_name, args.temp_dir)
```
`get_pkg_file` uses `subprocess.run(cmd, shell=True).returncode == 0`. This is synchronous and has no timeout. If `smbclient` hangs, the whole script hangs.

I'll add a timeout to `get_pkg_file` and ensure all `print` calls are converted to `log` calls.

## Assistant (Build · gemma-4-31b-it · 82.6s)

_Thinking:_

The log file confirms that the script is indeed hanging.
It stops at:
`[82/98] Processing: UP8802-CUSA02084_00-RB4RBNRERELEASES-A0000-V0100.pkg`

It doesn't even reach the `[1/4] Extracting` part for that PKG.
Wait, look at the log again:
`[82/98] Processing: UP8802-CUSA02084_00-RB4RBNRERELEASES-A0000-V0100.pkg` is the last line.
The next step in `extract_songdta_from_pkg` is:
`print(f"\t\t[1/4] Extracting: {pkg_name}")`
But the log only has the `Processing: ...` line from the `main` loop.

This means it's hanging right at the start of `extract_songdta_from_pkg`.
The first thing `extract_songdta_from_pkg` does is:
`pkg_name = os.path.basename(pkg_path)`
`print(f"\t\t[1/4] Extracting: {pkg_name}")`

But wait, the log only uses the `log()` function.
In `extract_songdta_from_pkg`, it uses `print()`.
I replaced `print` with `log` in `main`, but I didn't replace them in `extract_songdta_from_pkg`.

However, the `print` statements in `extract_songdta_from_pkg` should still appear in the console.
The log file only contains what was sent to `log()`.

If the log stops at `[82/98] Processing: ...`, it means it entered `extract_songdta_from_pkg` and then stopped.

Wait, if the user says it "stops around pkg #28 or 29", and now it's at #82... it's moving.
But it still hangs.

Let's look at the `extract_songdta_from_pkg` function:
```python
def extract_songdta_from_pkg(pkg_path, source_name, temp_dir, empty_baseline=None):
    pkg_name = os.path.basename(pkg_path)
    print(f"\t\t[1/4] Extracting: {pkg_name}")
    sys.stdout.flush()
    ...
```

If it's hanging *before* the first `print`, it's very strange.
Unless... `os.path.basename(pkg_path)` is hanging? Unlikely.

Maybe the `run_cmd` for `pkg_extractinnerpfs` is hanging?
`run_cmd(f'DOTNET_SYSTEM_GLOBALIZATION_INVARIANT=1 PkgTool.Core pkg_extractinnerpfs "{pkg_path}" {pfs_file}', show_output=True, indent="\t\t", timeout=600)`

If it hangs there, the `show_output=True` should be printing things to the console.
The user says "the output stops at a random character". This often happens when there's a binary output or a encoding issue, or when the process is killed.

I've already added `errors='replace'` to the decoder.

One more thing: the `temp_dir` might be filling up?
`df -h` showed 42G available on overlay.
But the PKGs are large.
The script deletes `work_dir` in a `finally` block.

Wait, if the process is killed by OOM, the `finally` block might not run if it's a `SIGKILL`.
But `top` shows plenty of memory (3.6G free, 3.9G used).

Let's try to wrap the `extract_songdta_from_pkg` call in a way that we can see exactly where it's hanging.
I will replace all `print` in `extract_songdta_from_pkg` with `log`.

**Tool: edit**

## Assistant (Build · gemma-4-31b-it · 21.4s)

_Thinking:_

The output is truncated again at the same point (PKG #40).
Crucially, the tool says "The tool call succeeded". This means the bash process returned.
But as I checked before, `rb4_custom_songs.json` is missing, which means the script did not complete.

If the tool call "succeeded" but the script didn't finish, it means the script exited without returning a non-zero exit code, or it was killed in a way that didn't return an error to the bash shell.

Actually, if the script is killed by OOM (Out of Memory), it might return a specific exit code.

## Goal

Extract and identify all Rock Band 4 song metadata from PS4 PKG files to match the PS4's reported total of 4,084 songs. Currently, there is a significant gap between the extracted count and the target.

## Instructions

- **SMB Sources**: 
    - DLC PKGs: `//192.168.100.135/incoming/temp/Rb4Dlc`
    - Game PKGs: `//192.168.100.135/incoming/temp/rb4gamepkgs`
- **Storage Constraints**: Process only one PKG at a time. Delete local PKGs and extracted contents immediately after processing to prevent disk space exhaustion.
- **Baseline Mapping**: Use `RB4/rb4_empty_songs_full.json` to map songs with "empty" (all zeros) `.songdta_ps4` files back to their probable artist and title.
- **Environment**: All .NET tools must be run with `DOTNET_SYSTEM_GLOBALIZATION_INVARIANT=1`.
- **Memory Management**: Keep `.ai_memory/rb4-libforge-extraction/` updated with the current plan and status.

## Discoveries

- **Console Hangs**: The `rb4_songlist_generator.py` script frequently hangs or stops outputting to the console around PKG #28-40 or #83. This appears to be related to how `subprocess.Popen` handles certain characters in the output stream.
- **Base Game Format**: The Game v1.00 PKG extracts into `.ark` files rather than a standard PFS image, meaning `.songdta_ps4` files are not immediately accessible via `PkgTool.Core`.
- **Corruption/Encryption**: The Game Update PKG (v2.21) triggers a `System.Exception: inode 0 is corrupt` error during PFS extraction, suggesting a format incompatibility or corruption.
- **Baseline Path**: The empty songs baseline was previously looked for in the root `/workspace/`, but it is actually located in `/workspace/RB4/rb4_empty_songs_full.json`.

## Accomplished

- **Logging & Stability Improvements**:
    - Replaced most `print` statements with a `log()` function that writes to both the console and a persistent log file in `/workspace/rb4_temp/` to track progress even if the console hangs.
    - Updated `subprocess.Popen` to read output in binary mode with manual UTF-8 decoding (`errors='replace'`) to prevent encoding-related hangs.
    - Implemented strict timeouts in `run_cmd` to prevent the script from waiting indefinitely on hung processes.
- **Path Corrections**: Updated the generator script to use the correct path for `rb4_empty_songs_full.json`.
- **Environment**: Verified the .NET environment and basic SMB connectivity.

## Relevant files / directories

- `/workspace/RB4/scripts/rb4_songlist_generator.py` - Main orchestration script.
- `/workspace/RB4/scripts/extract_binary_dta.py` - Python parser for `.songdta_ps4` files.
- `/workspace/RB4/scripts/smb_pkg_finder.py` - Logic for listing and fetching PKGs via `smbclient`.
- `/workspace/RB4/rb4_empty_songs_full.json` - Metadata baseline for "empty" binary files.
- `/workspace/RB4/rb4_custom_songs.json` - The resulting extracted song list.
- `/workspace/rb4_temp/` - Temporary directory for PKG extraction and log files.
- `/workspace/.devcontainer/rb4_dlc_config.sh` - SMB server and share configuration.

## Next Steps

1. **Resolve Full Run Hang**: Ensure the `rb4_songlist_generator.py` can successfully complete a `--no-incremental` run of all 98 DLC PKGs without hanging. Monitor the log files to identify the exact PKG causing the stall.
2. **Ark File Extraction**: Investigate a method to extract `.songdta_ps4` files from the `.ark` archives found in the Game v1.00 PKG.
3. **Fix Update PKG Crash**: Determine why the v2.21 PKG reports a corrupt inode and find a way to extract its contents.
4. **Final Reconciliation**: Once all sources are processed, compare the final count against the 4,084 target.

```
122: def run_cmd(cmd, check=True, capture=True, show_output=False, indent="\t\t", timeout=None):
123:     """Run command and return output. Use show_output=True for realtime feedback with indent."""
124:     import subprocess
125:     import threading
126:     
127:     if show_output:
128:         process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, shell=True, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=False, bufsize=1)
129:         
130:         def stream_output(stream):
131:             try:
132:                 for line in stream:
133:                     decoded_line = line.decode('utf-8', errors='replace').rstrip()
134:                     print(f"{indent}{decoded_line}")
135:                     sys.stdout.flush()
136:             except Exception as e:
137:                 print(f"{indent}Error reading output: {e}")
138:         
139:         thread = threading.Thread(target=stream_output, args=(process.stdout,))
140:         thread.daemon = True
141:         thread.start()
142:         
143:         try:
144:             process.wait(timeout=timeout)
145:         except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
146:             process.kill()
147:             raise RuntimeError(f"Command timed out after {timeout} seconds: {cmd}")
148:             
149:         thread.join(timeout=5)
150:         
151:         if check and process.returncode != 0:
152:             raise RuntimeError(f"Command failed: {cmd}")
153:         return ""
154:     
155:     result = subprocess.run(cmd, shell=True, capture_output=capture, text=True, timeout=timeout)
156:     if check and result.returncode != 0:
157:         print(f"ERROR: {cmd}")
158:         print(f"stdout: {result.stdout}")
159:         print(f"stderr: {result.stderr}")
160:         raise RuntimeError(f"Command failed: {cmd}")
161:     return result.stdout if capture else ""

414:             continue
415:     
416:     log(f"\nExtracted {len(all_songs)} songs from {len(pkg_files)} PKGs")
417:     
418:     # Load existing songs if incremental mode and file exists
419:     if args.incremental and os.path.exists(args.output_json):
420:         with open(args.output_json) as f:
421:             existing = json.load(f)
422:         # Merge (new songs will override duplicates)
423:         existing_dict = {(s['artist'], s['title']): s for s in existing}
424:         for song in all_songs:
425:             key = (song['artist'], song['title'])
426:             existing_dict[key] = song
427:         all_songs = list(existing_dict.values())
428:         log(f"Merged with existing: {len(all_songs)} total songs")
429:     
430:     # Filter out garbage entries
431:     valid_songs = [s for s in all_songs if s.get('title') or s.get('artist')]
432:     garbage = len(all_songs) - len(valid_songs)
433:     if garbage > 0:
434:         log(f"Filtered out {garbage} garbage entries")
435:     
436:     # NEW: Track empty songs separately (these are REAL songs with unparseable metadata)
437:     # They have no title/artist because .songdta_ps4 contains only zeros
438:     empty_songs = [s for s in all_songs if not s.get('title') and not s.get('artist')]
439:     if empty_songs:
440:         empty_output = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(args.output_json), 'empty_songs.json')
441:         with open(empty_output, 'w') as f:
442:             json.dump(empty_songs, f, indent=2)
443:         log(f"Saved {len(empty_songs)} empty songs (unparseable metadata) to: {empty_output}")
444:     
445:     # Record update for history (always, to show in output)
446:     # Track which songs are new in this run
447:     existing_set = set()
448:     if os.path.exists(args.output_json):
449:         with open(args.output_json) as f:
450:             existing = json.load(f)
451:             existing_set = {(s['artist'], s['title']) for s in existing}
452:     
453:     new_only = [s for s in valid_songs if (s['artist'], s['title']) not in existing_set]
454:     if new_only:
455:         record_update(new_only, len(valid_songs))
456:         log(f"Recorded {len(new_only)} new songs in update history")
457:     elif len(all_songs) > 0:
458:         # Even if no truly new songs, record this run (for --no-incremental)
459:         record_update(valid_songs, len(valid_songs))
460:         log(f"Recorded {len(valid_songs)} songs in update history (full rebuild)")
461:     
462:     # Write JSON
463:     with open(args.output_json, 'w') as f:
464:         json.dump(valid_songs, f, indent=2)
465:     log(f"Written: {args.output_json}")
466:     
467:     # Check for issues
468:     zero_dur = [s for s in valid_songs if s.get('durationMs', 0) == 0]
469:     if zero_dur:
470:         log(f"\n⚠️  Songs with durationMs=0: {len(zero_dur)}")
471:     
472:     # Generate song lists
473:     log(f"\nGenerating song lists...")
474:     run_cmd(f'cd /workspace/RB4 && node generate_rb4_song_list.js --baseline {args.baseline} --custom {args.output_json} --processed {PROCESSED_PKGS_FILE}')
475:     
476:     log("\n✅ Pipeline complete!")
477:     log(f"Processed PKGs saved to: {PROCESSED_PKGS_FILE}")
478: 
479: 
480: if __name__ == '__main__':
481:     main()

(End of file - total 481 lines)
</content>
```

## Assistant (Build · gemma-4-31b-it · 10.6s)

_Thinking:_

Wait, it DID extract the files!

The `Bash` tool returned a result, and `ls -R` shows that it extracted a lot of folders and files, including `.songdta_ps4` files.

So `pfs_extract` worked, it just took a long time and the output was maybe not flushed or it finished and I just didn't see the "Done" message.

So the problem isn't a hang in the sense of an infinite loop, but rather a very slow process for large PKGs.

The `rb4_songlist_generator.py` script has a timeout of 600 seconds (10 minutes) for `pfs_extract`.

For a 4.9 GB PFS, 10 minutes might not be enough.

I should increase the timeout in `rb4_songlist_generator.py`.

Let's check the timeout in the script.

**Tool: read**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "/workspace/RB4/scripts/rb4_songlist_generator.py"
}
```

**Output:**

```
50:             with open(baseline_path) as f:

53:                 return {s['short_filename']: {'title': s.get('probable_title'), 'artist': s.get('probable_artist')} 
54:                         for s in data if 'short_filename' in s}

83: def record_update(new_songs, total_songs_count):
84:     """Record this update in history."""
85:     history = load_update_history()
86:     from datetime import datetime
87:     import os
88:     # Respect TZ environment variable for local timezone

97:     # Keep last 10 updates
98:     if len(history) > 10:
99:         history = history[-10:]
100:     save_update_history(history)

102: # Package source mapping
103: def get_pkg_source(pkg_path):
104:     """Extract source name from PKG filename."""
105:     basename = os.path.basename(pkg_path)
106:     if "CREQ" in basename:
107:         return "custom"
108:     elif "GDRB" in basename or "GREENDAY" in basename:
109:         return "greenday"
110:     elif "RB2" in basename:
111:         return "rb2"
112:     elif "DELISTED" in basename:
113:         return "delisted"
114:     elif "UNRELEASED" in basename or "DLCUNRELEASED" in basename:
115:         return "unreleased"
116:     elif "SEASON" in basename:
117:         return "rb4"
118:     elif "UNEXPORTABLE" in basename:
119:         return "unexportable"
120:     return "unknown"
121: 
122: def run_cmd(cmd, check=True, capture=True, show_output=False, indent="\t\t", timeout=None):
123:     """Run command and return output. Use show_output=True for realtime feedback with indent."""
124:     import subprocess
125:     import threading
126:     
127:     if show_output:
128:         process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, shell=True, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=False, bufsize=1)
129:         
130:         def stream_output(stream):
131:             try:
132:                 for line in stream:
133:                     decoded_line = line.decode('utf-8', errors='replace').rstrip()
134:                     print(f"{indent}{decoded_line}")
135:                     sys.stdout.flush()
136:             except Exception as e:
137:                 print(f"{indent}Error reading output: {e}")
138:         
139:         thread = threading.Thread(target=stream_output, args=(process.stdout,))
140:         thread.daemon = True
141:         thread.start()
142:         
143:         try:
144:             process.wait(timeout=timeout)
145:         except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
146:             process.kill()
147:             raise RuntimeError(f"Command timed out after {timeout} seconds: {cmd}")
148:             
149:         thread.join(timeout=5)
150:         
151:         if check and process.returncode != 0:
152:             raise RuntimeError(f"Command failed: {cmd}")
153:         return ""
154:     
155:     result = subprocess.run(cmd, shell=True, capture_output=capture, text=True, timeout=timeout)
156:     if check and result.returncode != 0:
157:         print(f"ERROR: {cmd}")
158:         print(f"stdout: {result.stdout}")
159:         print(f"stderr: {result.stderr}")
160:         raise RuntimeError(f"Command failed: {cmd}")
161:     return result.stdout if capture else ""
162: 
163: def extract_songdta_from_pkg(pkg_path, source_name, temp_dir, empty_baseline=None):
164:     """Extract only .songdta_ps4 files from a PKG using two-step extraction."""
165:     pkg_name = os.path.basename(pkg_path)
166:     log(f"\t\t[1/4] Extracting: {pkg_name}")
167:     sys.stdout.flush()
168:     
169:     basename = pkg_name.replace('.pkg', '')
170:     work_dir = os.path.join(temp_dir, 'pfs_extract_' + basename)
171:     pfs_file = os.path.join(work_dir, "inner.pfs")
172:     pfs_extract_dir = os.path.join(work_dir, "pfs_contents")
173:     
174:     os.makedirs(work_dir, exist_ok=True)
175:     
176:     try:
177:         # Step 1: Extract inner PFS image
178:         log(f"\t\t[2/4] Extracting PFS image...")
179:         sys.stdout.flush()
180:         run_cmd(f'DOTNET_SYSTEM_GLOBALIZATION_INVARIANT=1 PkgTool.Core pkg_extractinnerpfs "{pkg_path}" {pfs_file}', show_output=True, indent="\t\t", timeout=600)
181:         
182:         # Step 2: Extract PFS contents
183:         log(f"\t\t[3/4] Extracting song data from PFS...")
184:         sys.stdout.flush()
185:         try:
186:             run_cmd(f'DOTNET_SYSTEM_GLOBALIZATION_INVARIANT=1 PkgTool.Core pfs_extract {pfs_file} {pfs_extract_dir}', show_output=True, indent="\t\t\t", timeout=600)
187:         except RuntimeError:
188:             log("\t\tFirst attempt failed, retrying...")
189:             run_cmd(f'DOTNET_SYSTEM_GLOBALIZATION_INVARIANT=1 PkgTool.Core pfs_extract {pfs_file} {pfs_extract_dir}', show_output=True, indent="\t\t\t", timeout=600)
190:         
191:         # Find all .songdta_ps4 files
192:         songdta_files = []
193:         for root, dirs, files in os.walk(pfs_extract_dir):
194:             for f in files:
195:                 if f.endswith('.songdta_ps4'):
196:                     songdta_files.append(os.path.join(root, f))
197:         
198:         if not songdta_files:
199:             log(f"\t\tNo songdta files found!")
200:             return []
201:         
202:         # Extract metadata using Python script
203:         temp_output = os.path.join(temp_dir, f'metadata_{basename}.json')
204:         files_arg = ' '.join(f'"{f}"' for f in songdta_files)
205:         run_cmd(f'cd /workspace && python3 RB4/scripts/extract_binary_dta.py {files_arg} {temp_output}', show_output=True, indent="\t\t", timeout=300)
206:         
207:         # Load and tag with source
208:         with open(temp_output) as f:
209:             songs = json.load(f)
210:         
211:         # Handle empty songs using baseline if provided
212:         if empty_baseline:
213:             for song in songs:
214:                 # Use _debug_file (filename) as the key for the baseline mapping
215:                 filename = song.get('_debug_file', '')
216:                 short_name = filename.replace('.songdta_ps4', '')
217:                 
218:                 if not song.get('artist') or song.get('artist') == 'Unknown':
219:                     if short_name in empty_baseline:
220:                         baseline_info = empty_baseline[short_name]
221:                         # Use baseline if current is empty or 'Unknown'
222:                         current_title = song.get('title')
223:                         current_artist = song.get('artist')
224:                         
225:                         if not current_title or current_title == short_name:
226:                             song['title'] = baseline_info.get('title') or current_title
227:                         if not current_artist or current_artist == 'Unknown':
228:                             song['artist'] = baseline_info.get('artist') or current_artist
229:     
230:         for song in songs:
231:             binary_source = song.get('source', '')
232:             use_pkg_source = (
233:                 source_name not in ('unknown', 'Custom') or 
234:                 binary_source in ('Custom', 'unknown', '')
235:             )
236:             if use_pkg_source:
237:                 song['source'] = source_name
238:         
239:         log(f"\t\tExtracted {len(songs)} songs")
240:         return songs
241:         
242:     finally:
243:         # Clean up to free disk space
244:         log(f"\t\t[4/4] Cleaning up extraction files...")
245:         sys.stdout.flush()
246:         shutil.rmtree(work_dir, ignore_errors=True)
247:         log(f"\t✓ Done: {pkg_name}")
248: 
249: 
250: def main():
251:     parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
252:         description='Extract song metadata from Rock Band 4 PKG files',
253:         formatter_class=argparse.RawDescriptionHelpFormatter,
254:         epilog='''
255: Examples:
256:   # Extract from local PKG directory (default paths)
257:   python3 RB4/scripts/rb4_extract_songs.py
258: 
259:   # Extract from network share mounted locally
260:   python3 RB4/scripts/rb4_extract_songs.py --pkg-dir /mnt/rb4dlc
261: 
262:   # Force full re-extraction (disable incremental mode)
263:   python3 RB4/scripts/rb4_extract_songs.py --pkg-dir /mnt/rb4dlc --no-incremental
264: 
265:   # Use custom temp directory
266:   python3 RB4/scripts/rb4_extract_songs.py --pkg-dir /mnt/rb4dlc --temp-dir /tmp/rb4_extract
267: '''
268:     )
269:     parser.add_argument('--pkg-dir', default=DEFAULT_PKG_DIR,
270:                         help=f'Directory containing PKG files (default: {DEFAULT_PKG_DIR})')
271:     parser.add_argument('--temp-dir', default=DEFAULT_TEMP_DIR,
272:                         help=f'Temporary directory for extraction (default: {DEFAULT_TEMP_DIR})')
273:     parser.add_argument('--output-json', default=DEFAULT_OUTPUT_JSON,
274:                         help=f'Output JSON file for custom songs (default: {DEFAULT_OUTPUT_JSON})')
275:     parser.add_argument('--songlist-dir', default=DEFAULT_SONGLIST_DIR,
276:                         help=f'Output directory for song lists (default: {DEFAULT_SONGLIST_DIR})')
277:     parser.add_argument('--baseline', default='/workspace/RB4/rb4songlistWithRivals.txt',
278:                         help='Baseline song list file')
279:     parser.add_argument('--incremental', action='store_true', default=True,
280:                         help='Skip already-processed PKGs (default: enabled)')
281:     parser.add_argument('--no-incremental', action='store_false', dest='incremental',
282:                         help='Disable incremental mode - re-process all PKGs')
283:     parser.add_argument('-v', '--verbose', action='store_true',
284:                         help='Verbose output')
285:     parser.add_argument('--smb', action='store_true',
286:                         help='PKGs are on SMB share (use smbclient to access)')
287:     parser.add_argument('--log', default=None,
288:                         help='Log file path (default: temp_dir/metadata_<timestamp>.log)')
289:     
290:     args = parser.parse_args()
291:     
292:     # Create temp directory
293:     os.makedirs(args.temp_dir, exist_ok=True)
294:     
295:     global LOG_FILE
296:     if args.log:
297:         LOG_FILE = args.log
298:     else:
299:         ts = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
300:         LOG_FILE = os.path.join(args.temp_dir, f'rb4_extract_{ts}.log')
301:     log(f"Logging to: {LOG_FILE}")
302:     log(f"Started at {datetime.now().isoformat()}")
303:     
304:     # Reset if --no-incremental (fresh run)
305:     if not args.incremental:
306:         log("Full rebuild mode - clearing previous state...")
307:         for f in [PROCESSED_PKGS_FILE, UPDATE_HISTORY_FILE, args.output_json]:
308:             if os.path.exists(f):
309:                 os.remove(f)
310:         # Clear output directory BEFORE generating
311:         if os.path.exists(args.songlist_dir):
312:             for f in os.listdir(args.songlist_dir):
313:                 os.remove(os.path.join(args.songlist_dir, f))
314:     
315:     # Find all PKG files
316:     empty_baseline = load_empty_songs_baseline()
317:     if empty_baseline:
318:         log(f"Loaded empty songs baseline with {len(empty_baseline)} entries")
319: 
320:     if args.smb:
321:         # Use smbclient to list PKGs from SMB share
322:         log("Accessing PKGs via SMB...")
323:         sys.path.insert(0, '/workspace/RB4/scripts')
324:         from smb_pkg_finder import list_pkgs as smb_list_pkgs
325:         pkg_names = smb_list_pkgs()
326:         pkg_files = pkg_names  # Store just names, we'll fetch one at a time
327:     else:
328:         # Local directory - filter out macOS hidden files (starting with ._)
329:         if not os.path.isdir(args.pkg_dir):
330:             log(f"ERROR: PKG directory not found: {args.pkg_dir}")
331:             sys.exit(1)
332:         
333:         pkg_files = [
334:             os.path.join(args.pkg_dir, f) 
335:             for f in os.listdir(args.pkg_dir) 
336:             if f.endswith('.pkg') and not f.startswith('._')
337:         ]
338:     
339:     if not pkg_files:
340:         log(f"No .pkg files found in {args.pkg_dir}")
341:         sys.exit(1)
342:     
343:     log(f"Found {len(pkg_files)} PKG files in {args.pkg_dir}")
344:     
345:     # Load processed PKGs for incremental mode
346:     processed = load_processed_pkgs() if args.incremental else set()
347:     log(f"Incremental mode: {'enabled' if args.incremental else 'disabled'}")
348:     if processed:
349:         log(f"  Already processed: {len(processed)} PKGs")
350:     
351:     # Filter out already-processed PKGs
352:     if args.incremental:
353:         new_pkgs = [p for p in pkg_files if os.path.basename(p) not in processed]
354:         skipped = len(pkg_files) - len(new_pkgs)
355:         if skipped > 0:
356:             log(f"  Skipping {skipped} already-processed PKGs")
357:         pkg_files = new_pkgs
358:     
359:     if not pkg_files:
360:         log("No new PKGs to process.")
361:         log("\nGenerating song lists from existing data...")
362:         run_cmd(f'cd /workspace/RB4 && node generate_rb4_song_list.js --baseline {args.baseline} --custom {args.output_json} --processed {PROCESSED_PKGS_FILE}')
363:         log("✅ Done!")
364:         sys.exit(0)
365:     
366:     log(f"Processing {len(pkg_files)} new PKGs...")
367:     
368:     all_songs = []
369:     total_pkgs = len(pkg_files)
370:     
371:     for idx, pkg_path in enumerate(sorted(pkg_files), 1):
372:         source = get_pkg_source(pkg_path)
373:         pkg_name = os.path.basename(pkg_path)
374:         
375:         # For SMB mode: fetch one file at a time
376:         if args.smb:
377:             log(f"[{idx}/{total_pkgs}] Fetching: {pkg_name}")
378:             sys.stdout.flush()
379:             
380:             # Fetch from SMB to temp dir
381:             sys.path.insert(0, '/workspace/RB4/scripts')
382:             from smb_pkg_finder import get_pkg_file
383:             success = get_pkg_file(pkg_name, args.temp_dir)
384:             
385:             if not success:
386:                 log(f"  ERROR: Failed to fetch {pkg_name} from SMB")
387:                 continue
388:             
389:             # Use the fetched file
390:             pkg_path = os.path.join(args.temp_dir, pkg_name)
391:         
392:         log(f"[{idx}/{total_pkgs}] Processing: {pkg_name}")
393:         sys.stdout.flush()
394:         
395:         try:
396:             songs = extract_songdta_from_pkg(pkg_path, source, args.temp_dir, empty_baseline)
397:             all_songs.extend(songs)
398:             
399:             # For SMB mode: clean up immediately after processing to free space
400:             if args.smb and os.path.exists(pkg_path):
401:                 os.remove(pkg_path)
402:                 print(f"\tCleaned up {pkg_name} to free space")
403:             
404:             # Mark as processed
405:             processed.add(pkg_name)
406:             save_processed_pkgs(processed)
407:             
408:             pct = int(idx / total_pkgs * 100)
409:             print(f"Progress: {pct}% ({idx}/{total_pkgs} PKGs) | Total songs: {len(all_songs)}")
410:             sys.stdout.flush()
411:             
412:         except Exception as e:
413:             log(f"ERROR processing {pkg_name}: {e}")
414:             continue
415:     
416:     log(f"\nExtracted {len(all_songs)} songs from {len(pkg_files)} PKGs")
417:     
418:     # Load existing songs if incremental mode and file exists
419:     if args.incremental and os.path.exists(args.output_json):
420:         with open(args.output_json) as f:
421:             existing = json.load(f)
422:         # Merge (new songs will override duplicates)
423:         existing_dict = {(s['artist'], s['title']): s for s in existing}
424:         for song in all_songs:
425:             key = (song['artist'], song['title'])
426:             existing_dict[key] = song
427:         all_songs = list(existing_dict.values())
428:         log(f"Merged with existing: {len(all_songs)} total songs")
429:     
430:     # Filter out garbage entries
431:     valid_songs = [s for s in all_songs if s.get('title') or s.get('artist')]
432:     garbage = len(all_songs) - len(valid_songs)
433:     if garbage > 0:
434:         log(f"Filtered out {garbage} garbage entries")
435:     
436:     # NEW: Track empty songs separately (these are REAL songs with unparseable metadata)
437:     # They have no title/artist because .songdta_ps4 contains only zeros
438:     empty_songs = [s for s in all_songs if not s.get('title') and not s.get('artist')]
439:     if empty_songs:
440:         empty_output = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(args.output_json), 'empty_songs.json')
441:         with open(empty_output, 'w') as f:
442:             json.dump(empty_songs, f, indent=2)
443:         log(f"Saved {len(empty_songs)} empty songs (unparseable metadata) to: {empty_output}")
444:     
445:     # Record update for history (always, to show in output)
446:     # Track which songs are new in this run
447:     existing_set = set()
448:     if os.path.exists(args.output_json):
449:         with open(args.output_json) as f:
450:             existing = json.load(f)
451:             existing_set = {(s['artist'], s['title']) for s in existing}
452:     
453:     new_only = [s for s in valid_songs if (s['artist'], s['title']) not in existing_set]
454:     if new_only:
455:         record_update(new_only, len(valid_songs))
456:         log(f"Recorded {len(new_only)} new songs in update history")
457:     elif len(all_songs) > 0:
458:         # Even if no truly new songs, record this run (for --no-incremental)
459:         record_update(valid_songs, len(valid_songs))
460:         log(f"Recorded {len(valid_songs)} songs in update history (full rebuild)")
461:     
462:     # Write JSON
463:     with open(args.output_json, 'w') as f:
464:         json.dump(valid_songs, f, indent=2)
465:     log(f"Written: {args.output_json}")
466:     
467:     # Check for issues
468:     zero_dur = [s for s in valid_songs if s.get('durationMs', 0) == 0]
469:     if zero_dur:
470:         log(f"\n⚠️  Songs with durationMs=0: {len(zero_dur)}")

472:     # Generate song lists
```

```
102: # Package source mapping
103: def get_pkg_source(pkg_path):
104:     """Extract source name from PKG filename."""
105:     basename = os.path.basename(pkg_path)
106:     if "CREQ" in basename:
107:         return "custom"
108:     elif "GDRB" in basename or "GREENDAY" in basename:
109:         return "greenday"
110:     elif "RB2" in basename:
111:         return "rb2"
112:     elif "DELISTED" in basename:
113:         return "delisted"
114:     elif "UNRELEASED" in basename or "DLCUNRELEASED" in basename:
115:         return "unreleased"
116:     elif "SEASON" in basename:
117:         return "rb4"
118:     elif "UNEXPORTABLE" in basename:
119:         return "unexportable"
120:     return "unknown"

122: def run_cmd(cmd, check=True, capture=True, show_output=False, indent="\t\t", timeout=None):
123:     """Run command and return output. Use show_output=True for realtime feedback with indent."""
124:     import subprocess
125:     import threading
126:     
127:     if show_output:
128:         process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, shell=True, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=False, bufsize=1)
129:         
130:         def stream_output(stream):
131:             try:
132:                 for line in stream:
133:                     decoded_line = line.decode('utf-8', errors='replace').rstrip()
134:                     print(f"{indent}{decoded_line}")
135:                     sys.stdout.flush()
136:             except Exception as e:
137:                 print(f"{indent}Error reading output: {e}")
138:         
139:         thread = threading.Thread(target=stream_output, args=(process.stdout,))
140:         thread.daemon = True
141:         thread.start()
142:         
143:         try:
144:             process.wait(timeout=timeout)
145:         except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
146:             process.kill()
147:             raise RuntimeError(f"Command timed out after {timeout} seconds: {cmd}")
148:             
149:         thread.join(timeout=5)
150:         
151:         if check and process.returncode != 0:
152:             raise RuntimeError(f"Command failed: {cmd}")
153:         return ""
154:     
155:     result = subprocess.run(cmd, shell=True, capture_output=capture, text=True, timeout=timeout)
156:     if check and result.returncode != 0:
157:         print(f"ERROR: {cmd}")
158:         print(f"stdout: {result.stdout}")
159:         print(f"stderr: {result.stderr}")
160:         raise RuntimeError(f"Command failed: {cmd}")
161:     return result.stdout if capture else ""

163: def extract_songdta_from_pkg(pkg_path, source_name, temp_dir, empty_baseline=None):
164:     """Extract only .songdta_ps4 files from a PKG using two-step extraction."""
165:     pkg_name = os.path.basename(pkg_path)

168:

189:             run_cmd(f'DOTNET_SYSTEM_GLOBALIZATION_INVARIANT=1 PkgTool.Core pfs_extract {pfs_file} {pfs_extract_dir}', show_output=True, indent="\t\t\t", timeout=3600)
190:         except RuntimeError:
191:             log("\t\tFirst attempt failed, retrying...")
192:             run_cmd(f'DOTNET_SYSTEM_GLOBALIZATION_INVARIANT=1 PkgTool.Core pfs_extract {pfs_file} {pfs_extract_dir}', show_output=True, indent="\t\t\t", timeout=600)
193:         
194:         # Find all .songdta_ps4 files
195:         songdta_files = []
196:         for root, dirs, files in os.walk(pfs_extract_dir):

201:         if not songdta_files:

203:             return []
204:         
205:         # Extract metadata using Python script
206:         temp_output = os.path.join(temp_dir, f'metadata_{basename}.json')

210:         # Load and tag with source
211:         with open(temp_output) as f:
212:             songs = json.load(f)
213:         
214:         # Handle empty songs using baseline if provided
215:         if empty_baseline:
216:             for song in songs:
217:                 # Use _debug_file (filename) as the key for the baseline mapping
218:                 filename = song.get('_debug_file', '')
219:                 short_name = filename.replace('.songdta_ps4', '')
220:                 
221:                 if not song.get('artist') or song.get('artist') == 'Unknown':
222:                     if short_name in empty_baseline:
223:                         baseline_info = empty_baseline[short_name]
224:                         # Use baseline if current is empty or 'Unknown'
225:                         current_title = song.get('title')
226:                         current_artist = song.get('artist')
227:                         
228:                         if not current_title or current_title == short_name:

231:                             song['artist'] = baseline_info.get('artist') or current_artist
232:     
233:         for song in songs:

236:                 source_name not in ('unknown', 'Custom') or

238:             )
239:             if use_pkg_source:

253: def main():

269:   python3 RB4/scripts/rb4_extract_songs.py --pkg-dir /mnt/rb4dlc --temp-dir /tmp/rb4_extract
270: '''
271:     )
272:     parser.add_argument('--pkg-dir', default=DEFAULT_PKG_DIR,
273:                         help=f'Directory containing PKG files (default: {DEFAULT_PKG_DIR})')
274:     parser.add_argument('--temp-dir', default=DEFAULT_TEMP_DIR,
275:                         help=f'Temporary directory for extraction (default: {DEFAULT_TEMP_DIR})')
276:     parser.add_argument('--output-json', default=DEFAULT_OUTPUT_JSON,
277:                         help=f'Output JSON file for custom songs (default: {DEFAULT_OUTPUT_JSON})')
278:     parser.add_argument('--songlist-dir', default=DEFAULT_SONGLIST_DIR,
279:                         help=f'Output directory for song lists (default: {DEFAULT_SONGLIST_DIR})')
280:     parser.add_argument('--baseline', default='/workspace/RB4/rb4songlistWithRivals.txt',
281:                         help='Baseline song list file')
282:     parser.add_argument('--incremental', action='store_true', default=True,
283:                         help='Skip already-processed PKGs (default: enabled)')
284:     parser.add_argument('--no-incremental', action='store_false', dest='incremental',
285:                         help='Disable incremental mode - re-process all PKGs')
286:     parser.add_argument('-v', '--verbose', action='store_true',
287:                         help='Verbose output')
288:     parser.add_argument('--smb', action='store_true',
289:                         help='PKGs are on SMB share (use smbclient to access)')
290:     parser.add_argument('--log', default=None,
291:                         help='Log file path (default: temp_dir/metadata_<timestamp>.log)')
292:     
293:     args = parser.parse_args()
294:     
295:     # Create temp directory
296:     os.makedirs(args.temp_dir, exist_ok=True)
297:     
298:     global LOG_FILE
299:     if args.log:
300:         LOG_FILE = args.log
301:     else:
302:         ts = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
303:         LOG_FILE = os.path.join(args.temp_dir, f'rb4_extract_{ts}.log')
304:     log(f"Logging to: {LOG_FILE}")
305:     log(f"Started at {datetime.now().isoformat()}")
306:     
307:     # Reset if --no-incremental (fresh run)
308:     if not args.incremental:
309:         log("Full rebuild mode - clearing previous state...")
310:         for f in [PROCESSED_PKGS_FILE, UPDATE_HISTORY_FILE, args.output_json]:
311:             if os.path.exists(f):
312:                 os.remove(f)
313:         # Clear output directory BEFORE generating
314:         if os.path.exists(args.songlist_dir):
315:             for f in os.listdir(args.songlist_dir):
316:                 os.remove(os.path.join(args.songlist_dir, f))
317:     
318:     # Find all PKG files
319:     empty_baseline = load_empty_songs_baseline()
320:     if empty_baseline:
321:         log(f"Loaded empty songs baseline with {len(empty_baseline)} entries")
322: 
323:     if args.smb:
324:         # Use smbclient to list PKGs from SMB share
325:         log("Accessing PKGs via SMB...")
326:         sys.path.insert(0, '/workspace/RB4/scripts')
327:         from smb_pkg_finder import list_pkgs as smb_list_pkgs
328:         pkg_names = smb_list_pkgs()
329:         pkg_files = pkg_names  # Store just names, we'll fetch one at a time
330:     else:
331:         # Local directory - filter out macOS hidden files (starting with ._)
332:         if not os.path.isdir(args.pkg_dir):
333:             log(f"ERROR: PKG directory not found: {args.pkg_dir}")
334:             sys.exit(1)
335:         
336:         pkg_files = [
337:             os.path.join(args.pkg_dir, f) 
338:             for f in os.listdir(args.pkg_dir) 
339:             if f.endswith('.pkg') and not f.startswith('._')
340:         ]
341:     
342:     if not pkg_files:
343:         log(f"No .pkg files found in {args.pkg_dir}")
344:         sys.exit(1)
345:     
346:     log(f"Found {len(pkg_files)} PKG files in {args.pkg_dir}")
347:     
348:     # Load processed PKGs for incremental mode
349:     processed = load_processed_pkgs() if args.incremental else set()
350:     log(f"Incremental mode: {'enabled' if args.incremental else 'disabled'}")
351:     if processed:
352:         log(f"  Already processed: {len(processed)} PKGs")
353:     
354:     # Filter out already-processed PKGs
355:     if args.incremental:
356:         new_pkgs = [p for p in pkg_files if os.path.basename(p) not in processed]
357:         skipped = len(pkg_files) - len(new_pkgs)
358:         if skipped > 0:
359:             log(f"  Skipping {skipped} already-processed PKGs")
360:         pkg_files = new_pkgs
361:     
362:     if not pkg_files:
363:         log("No new PKGs to process.")
364:         log("\nGenerating song lists from existing data...")
365:         run_cmd(f'cd /workspace/RB4 && node generate_rb4_song_list.js --baseline {args.baseline} --custom {args.output_json} --processed {PROCESSED_PKGS_FILE}')
366:         log("✅ Done!")
367:         sys.exit(0)
368:     
369:     log(f"Processing {len(pkg_files)} new PKGs...")
370:     
371:     all_songs = []
372:     total_pkgs = len(pkg_files)
373:     
374:     for idx, pkg_path in enumerate(sorted(pkg_files), 1):
375:         source = get_pkg_source(pkg_path)
376:         pkg_name = os.path.basename(pkg_path)
377:         
378:         # For SMB mode: fetch one file at a time
379:         if args.smb:
380:             log(f"[{idx}/{total_pkgs}] Fetching: {pkg_name}")
381:             sys.stdout.flush()
382:             
383:             # Fetch from SMB to temp dir
384:             sys.path.insert(0, '/workspace/RB4/scripts')
385:             from smb_pkg_finder import get_pkg_file
386:             success = get_pkg_file(pkg_name, args.temp_dir)
387:             
388:             if not success:
389:                 log(f"  ERROR: Failed to fetch {pkg_name} from SMB")
390:                 continue
391:             
392:             # Use the fetched file
393:             pkg_path = os.path.join(args.temp_dir, pkg_name)
394:         
395:         log(f"[{idx}/{total_pkgs}] Processing: {pkg_name}")
396:         sys.stdout.flush()
397:         
398:         try:
399:             songs = extract_songdta_from_pkg(pkg_path, source, args.temp_dir, empty_baseline)
400:             all_songs.extend(songs)
401:             
402:             # For SMB mode: clean up immediately after processing to free space
403:             if args.smb and os.path.exists(pkg_path):
404:                 os.remove(pkg_path)
405:                 print(f"\tCleaned up {pkg_name} to free space")
406:             
407:             # Mark as processed
408:             processed.add(pkg_name)
409:             save_processed_pkgs(processed)
410:             
411:             pct = int(idx / total_pkgs * 100)
412:             print(f"Progress: {pct}% ({idx}/{total_pkgs} PKGs) | Total songs: {len(all_songs)}")
413:             sys.stdout.flush()
414:             
415:         except Exception as e:
416:             log(f"ERROR processing {pkg_name}: {e}")
417:             continue
418:     
419:     log(f"\nExtracted {len(all_songs)} songs from {len(pkg_files)} PKGs")
420:     
421:     # Load existing songs if incremental mode and file exists
422:     if args.incremental and os.path.exists(args.output_json):
423:         with open(args.output_json) as f:
424:             existing = json.load(f)
425:         # Merge (new songs will override duplicates)
426:         existing_dict = {(s['artist'], s['title']): s for s in existing}
427:         for song in all_songs:
428:             key = (song['artist'], song['title'])
429:             existing_dict[key] = song
430:         all_songs = list(existing_dict.values())
431:         log(f"Merged with existing: {len(all_songs)} total songs")
432:     
433:     # Filter out garbage entries
434:     valid_songs = [s for s in all_songs if s.get('title') or s.get('artist')]
435:     garbage = len(all_songs) - len(valid_songs)
436:     if garbage > 0:
437:         log(f"Filtered out {garbage} garbage entries")
438:     
439:     # NEW: Track empty songs separately (these are REAL songs with unparseable metadata)
440:     # They have no title/artist because .songdta_ps4 contains only zeros
441:     empty_songs = [s for s in all_songs if not s.get('title') and not s.get('artist')]
442:     if empty_songs:
443:         empty_output = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(args.output_json), 'empty_songs.json')
444:         with open(empty_output, 'w') as f:
445:             json.dump(empty_songs, f, indent=2)
446:         log(f"Saved {len(empty_songs)} empty songs (unparseable metadata) to: {empty_output}")
447:     
448:     # Record update for history (always, to show in output)
449:     # Track which songs are new in this run
450:     existing_set = set()
451:     if os.path.exists(args.output_json):
452:         with open(args.output_json) as f:
453:             existing = json.load(f)
454:             existing_set = {(s['artist'], s['title']) for s in existing}
455:     
456:     new_only = [s for s in valid_songs if (s['artist'], s['title']) not in existing_set]
457:     if new_only:
458:         record_update(new_only, len(valid_songs))
459:         log(f"Recorded {len(new_only)} new songs in update history")
460:     elif len(all_songs) > 0:
461:         # Even if no truly new songs, record this run (for --no-incremental)
462:         record_update(valid_songs, len(valid_songs))
463:         log(f"Recorded {len(valid_songs)} songs in update history (full rebuild)")
464:     
465:     # Write JSON
466:     with open(args.output_json, 'w') as f:
467:         json.dump(valid_songs, f, indent=2)
468:     log(f"Written: {args.output_json}")
469:     
470:     # Check for issues
471:     zero_dur = [s for s in valid_songs if s.get('durationMs', 0) == 0]
472:     if zero_dur:
473:         log(f"\n⚠️  Songs with durationMs=0: {len(zero_dur)}")
474:     
475:     # Generate song lists
476:     log(f"\nGenerating song lists...")
477:     run_cmd(f'cd /workspace/RB4 && node generate_rb4_song_list.js --baseline {args.baseline} --custom {args.output_json} --processed {PROCESSED_PKGS_FILE}')
478:     
479:     log("\n✅ Pipeline complete!")
480:     log(f"Processed PKGs saved to: {PROCESSED_PKGS_FILE}")

484:     main()
```

## Assistant (Build · gemma-4-31b-it · 13.7s)

_Thinking:_

It timed out again! But this time it's in `get_pkg_file` (fetching the PKG from SMB).

The PKG is `UP8802-CUSA02084_00-RBLEGACYDLCPASS1-A0000-V0100.pkg` and its size is 15.9 GB.

`smbclient` timed out after 1200 seconds (20 minutes). 15.9 GB at 11 MB/s should take about 1500 seconds.

So the timeout in `smb_pkg_finder.py` is too short for these huge PKGs.

I need to increase the timeout in `smb_pkg_finder.py`.

```json
{
  "filePath": "/workspace/RB4/scripts/smb_pkg_finder.py"
```

```
<type>file</type>
<content>1: #!/usr/bin/env python3
2: """
3: SMB Package Finder - uses smbclient to list/access PKG files without kernel mount
4: 
5: Reads config from .devcontainer/rb4_dlc_config.sh if available
6: """
7: import subprocess
8: import os
9: import tempfile
10: import shutil
11: 
12: # Load config from rb4_dlc_config.sh if it exists
13: SMB_SERVER = os.environ.get('SMB_SERVER', '192.168.100.135')
14: SMB_SHARE = os.environ.get('SMB_SHARE', 'incoming/temp/Rb4Dlc')
15: 
16: # Try to read from config file
17: config_path = '/workspace/.devcontainer/rb4_dlc_config.sh'
18: if os.path.exists(config_path):
19:     with open(config_path) as f:
20:         for line in f:
21:             line = line.strip()
22:             if line.startswith('SMB_SERVER='):
23:                 SMB_SERVER = line.split('=')[1].strip('"')
24:             elif line.startswith('SMB_SHARE='):
25:                 SMB_SHARE = line.split('=')[1].strip('"')
26: 
27: def list_pkgs():
28:     """List PKG files from SMB share"""
29:     # Parse SMB_SHARE - could be just "incoming" or "incoming/temp/Rb4Dlc"
30:     share_parts = SMB_SHARE.split('/')
31:     base_share = share_parts[0]  # e.g., "incoming"
32:     sub_path = '/'.join(share_parts[1:]) if len(share_parts) > 1 else ''  # e.g., "temp/Rb4Dlc"
33:     
34:     if sub_path:
35:         cmd = f'smbclient //{SMB_SERVER}/{base_share} -N -c "cd {sub_path}; ls"'
36:     else:
37:         cmd = f'smbclient //{SMB_SERVER}/{base_share} -N -c "ls"'
38:     
39:     result = subprocess.run(cmd, shell=True, capture_output=True, text=True)
40:     
41:     pkgs = []
42:     for line in result.stdout.split('\n'):
43:         # Match lines like: "  UP8802-...-V0100.pkg      A 2853699584"
44:         if (('UP8802-' in line or 'Rock.Band.4_' in line) and '.pkg' in line and not line.startswith('  ._')):
45:             parts = line.split()
46:             if parts:
47:                 pkgs.append(parts[0])
48:     
49:     # If still no PKGs, try the temp/Rb4Dlc path directly
50:     if not pkgs:
51:         cmd2 = f'smbclient //{SMB_SERVER}/incoming/temp/Rb4Dlc -N -c "ls"'
52:         result2 = subprocess.run(cmd2, shell=True, capture_output=True, text=True)
53:         for line in result2.stdout.split('\n'):
54:             if (('UP8802-' in line or 'Rock.Band.4_' in line) and '.pkg' in line and not line.startswith('  ._')):
55:                 parts = line.split()
56:                 if parts:
57:                     pkgs.append(parts[0])
58:     
59:     return pkgs
60: 
61: def get_pkg_file(pkg_name, dest_dir):
62:     """Copy a single PKG file from SMB share"""
63:     # Parse SMB_SHARE - could be just "incoming" or "incoming/temp/Rb4Dlc"
64:     share_parts = SMB_SHARE.split('/')
65:     base_share = share_parts[0]  # e.g., "incoming"
66:     sub_path = '/'.join(share_parts[1:]) if len(share_parts) > 1 else ''  # e.g., "temp/Rb4Dlc"
67:     
68:     if sub_path:
69:         cmd = f'smbclient //{SMB_SERVER}/{base_share} -N -c "cd {sub_path}; get {pkg_name} {dest_dir}/{pkg_name}"'
70:     else:
71:         cmd = f'smbclient //{SMB_SERVER}/{base_share} -N -c "get {pkg_name} {dest_dir}/{pkg_name}"'
72:     
73:     return subprocess.run(cmd, shell=True, timeout=1200).returncode == 0
74: 
75: if __name__ == '__main__':
76:     print("=== SMB PKG Files ===")
77:     pkgs = list_pkgs()
78:     print(f"Found {len(pkgs)} PKG files:")
79:     for p in pkgs[:10]:
80:         print(f"  {p}")
81:     if len(pkgs) > 10:
82:         print(f"  ... and {len(pkgs) - 10} more")

(End of file - total 82 lines)
```

```
<content>1: // Simple console app to extract song metadata from RB4 DLC PKGs
2: // Uses LibForge library to parse .songdta_ps4 files
3: 
4: using System;

11: {
12:     static void Main(string[] args)
13:     {
14:         if (args.Length < 2)
15:         {
16:             Console.WriteLine("Usage: ExtractTool <pkg_file> <output_dir>");

19: 
20:         string pkgPath = args[0];
```

## Assistant (Build · gemma-4-31b-it · 8.2s)

_Thinking:_

I'll check `ArkPackage.cs` again.

**Tool: read**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "/workspace/LibForge/Dependencies/GameArchives/Library/Ark/ArkPackage.cs"
```
