
**Output:**
```
<path>/workspace/LibForge/Dependencies/GameArchives/Library/Ark/ArkPackage.cs</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ﻿/*
2:  * ArkPackage.cs
3:  * 
4:  * Copyright (c) 2015,2016,2017 maxton. All rights reserved.
5:  *
6:  * This library is free software; you can redistribute it and/or
7:  * modify it under the terms of the GNU Lesser General Public
8:  * License as published by the Free Software Foundation; either
9:  * version 3.0 of the License, or (at your option) any later version.
10:  *
11:  * This library is distributed in the hope that it will be useful,
12:  * but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
13:  * MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the GNU
14:  * Lesser General Public License for more details.
15:  *
16:  * You should have received a copy of the GNU Lesser General Public
17:  * License along with this library; If not, see
18:  * <http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.
19:  */
20: using GameArchives.Common;
21: using System;
22: using System.IO;
23: 
24: namespace GameArchives.Ark
25: {
26:   /// <summary>
27:   /// Ark Package
28:   /// </summary>
29:   public class ArkPackage : AbstractPackage
30:   {
31:     readonly static uint HIGHEST_VERSION = 10;
32:     readonly static uint LOWEST_VERSION = 1;
33:     readonly static uint ARK = 0x4B5241;
34: 
35:     private ArkDirectory root;
36:     private Stream[] contentFiles;
37:     private Stream contentFileMeta;
38:     private long[] arkFileSizes;
39:     private long totalArkFileSizes;
40: 
41:     // used for parsing
42:     private long fileNameTableOffset;
43:     private long fileNameTableSize;
44:     private long numFileNames;
45: 
46:     public override string FileName { get; }
47:     public override IDirectory RootDirectory => root;
48:     public override long Size => contentFileMeta.Length;
49:     public override bool Writeable => false;
50:     public override Type FileType => typeof(OffsetFile);
51: 
52:     public static PackageTestResult IsArk(IFile fn)
53:     {
54:       if (!fn.Name.ToLower().EndsWith(".hdr") && !fn.Name.ToLower().EndsWith(".ark"))
55:         return PackageTestResult.NO;
56: 
57:       using (Stream s = fn.GetStream())
58:       {
59:         s.Position = 0;
60:         uint version = s.ReadUInt32LE();
61:         if (version == ARK) // header from Frequency
62:         {
63:           return PackageTestResult.YES;
64:         }
65:         if (version > HIGHEST_VERSION)
66:         {
67:           // hdr is encrypted, probably
68:           using (var decryptor = new HdrCryptStream(s))
69:           {
70:             version = decryptor.ReadUInt32LE();
71:           }
72:           if (version == 0xFFFFFFF5) version = 10;
73:           else if (version == 0xFFFFFFF6) version = 9;
74:           else if (version == 0xFFFFFFF7) version = 8; // Hopefully?
75:         }
76:         return version <= HIGHEST_VERSION 
77:           && version >= LOWEST_VERSION ? PackageTestResult.MAYBE : PackageTestResult.NO;
78:       }
79:     }
80: 
81:     public static ArkPackage OpenFile(IFile f)
82:     {
83:       return new ArkPackage(f);
84:     }
85: 
86:     /// <summary>
87:     /// Instantiate ark package file from input .hdr file.
88:     /// Note: will check for data files and throw exception if they're not found.
89:     /// </summary>
90:     /// <param name="pathToHdr">Full path to .hdr file</param>
91:     public ArkPackage(IFile hdrFile)
92:     {
93:       FileName = hdrFile.Name;
94:       using (var hdr = hdrFile.GetStream())
95:       {
96:         Stream actualHdr = hdr;
97:         uint version = hdr.ReadUInt32LE();
98:         if(version > HIGHEST_VERSION && version != ARK)
99:         {
100:           // hdr is encrypted, probably
101:           using (var decryptor = new HdrCryptStream(hdr))
102:           {
103:             if(decryptor.ReadInt32LE() < 0)
104:             {
105:               decryptor.xor = 0xFF;
106:             }
107:             decryptor.Position = 0;
108:             byte[] arr = new byte[decryptor.Length];
109:             decryptor.Read(arr, 0, (int)decryptor.Length);
110:             actualHdr = new MemoryStream(arr);
111:           }
112:           version = actualHdr.ReadUInt32LE();
113:         }
114:         if (version == ARK)
115:         {
116:           actualHdr.Close();
117:           readOldArkHeader(hdrFile);
118:         }
119:         else if (version <= HIGHEST_VERSION && version >= LOWEST_VERSION)
120:         {
121:           readHeader(actualHdr, hdrFile, version);
122:         }
123:         else
124:         {
125:           throw new NotSupportedException($"Given ark file is not supported. (version {version}).");
126:         }
127:       }
128:     }
129: 
130:     private void readHeader(Stream header, IFile hdrFile, uint version, bool brokenv4 = false)
131:     {
132:       root = new ArkDirectory(null, ROOT_DIR);
133:       if (version >= 6) // Versions 6,7 have some sort of hash/key at the beginning?
134:       {
135:         header.Seek(4 + 16, SeekOrigin.Current); // skip unknown data
136:       }
137: 
138:       if (version > 2)
139:       {
140:         // Version 3+: two counts of .ark files
141:         int numArks = header.ReadInt32LE();
142:         int numArks2 = header.ReadInt32LE();
143:         if (numArks != numArks2)
144:         {
145:           throw new InvalidDataException("Ark header appears to be invalid (.ark count mismatch).");
146:         }
147:         arkFileSizes = new long[numArks];
148:         for (var i = 0; i < numArks; i++)
149:         {
150:           // All versions except 4 use 32-bit file sizes.
151:           arkFileSizes[i] = (version == 4 ? header.ReadInt64LE() : header.ReadInt32LE());
152:           if (version == 4 && arkFileSizes[i] > UInt32.MaxValue)
153:           {
154:             // RB TrackPack Classic has a broken v4, really a v5 mixed with v3
155:             header.Position = 4;
156:             readHeader(header, hdrFile, 5, true);
157:             return;
158:           }
159:           totalArkFileSizes += arkFileSizes[i];
160:         }
161: 
162:         // Version 5+: List of .ark file paths (from root of game disc)
163:         if (version >= 5)
164:         {
165:           int numArkPaths = header.ReadInt32LE();
166:           if (numArkPaths != numArks)
167:           {
168:             throw new InvalidDataException("Ark header appears to be invalid (.ark count mismatch).");
169:           }
170:           contentFiles = new Stream[numArks];
171:           for (var i = 0; i < numArkPaths; i++)
172:           {
173:             IFile arkFile = hdrFile.Parent.GetFile(header.ReadLengthUTF8().Split('/').Last());
174:             if(version == 10)
175:             {
176:               var tmpStream = arkFile.GetStream();
177:               if (tmpStream.Length > 32)
178:               {
179:                 tmpStream.Seek(-32, SeekOrigin.End);
180: 
181:                 if (tmpStream.ReadASCIINullTerminated(32) == "mcnxyxcmvmcxyxcmskdldkjshagsdhfj")
182:                 {
183:                   contentFiles[i] = new ProtectedFileStream(tmpStream);
184:                   continue;
185:                 }
186:               }
187:               tmpStream.Close();
188:             }
189:             contentFiles[i] = arkFile.GetStream();
190:           }
191: 
192:           // Versions 6,7,9: appear to have checksums or something for each content file?
193:           if (version >= 6 && version <= 9)
194:           {
195:             uint numChecksums = header.ReadUInt32LE();
196:             header.Seek(4 * numChecksums, SeekOrigin.Current);
197:           }
198:         }
199:         else // Versions <5: Just infer the .ark paths based on the .hdr filename.
200:         {
201:           contentFiles = new Stream[numArks];
202:           for (var i = 0; i < numArks2; i++)
203:           {
204:             IFile arkFile = hdrFile.Parent.GetFile(hdrFile.Name.Substring(0, hdrFile.Name.Length - 4) + "_" + i + ".ark");
205:             contentFiles[i] = arkFile.GetStream();
206:           }
207:         }
208:         contentFileMeta = new MultiStream(contentFiles);
209: 
210:         // new in version 7+: some sort of string table with game-specific data
211:         if (version >= 7)
212:         {
213:           uint root_count = header.ReadUInt32LE();
214:           while (root_count-- > 0)
215:           {
216:             uint num_strs = header.ReadUInt32LE();
217:             while (num_strs-- > 0) // skip past strings because we don't need them.
218:               header.Seek(header.ReadUInt32LE(), SeekOrigin.Current);
219:           }
220:         }
221:         if (version < 8) // Gonna assume 8 has new file table
222:           readFileTable(header, version, brokenv4);
223:         else
224:           readNewFileTable(header, version < 10);
225:       }
226:       else if (version == 1 || version == 2)
227:       {
228:         // Version 1,2: Here be file records. Skip 'em for now.
229:         uint numRecords = header.ReadUInt32LE();
230:         header.Close();
231:         contentFileMeta = hdrFile.GetStream();
232:         contentFileMeta.Seek(8 + numRecords * 20, SeekOrigin.Begin);
233:         readFileTable(contentFileMeta, version, brokenv4);
234:       }
235:     }
236: 
237:     // "ARK" files have a completely different header
238:     private void readOldArkHeader(IFile hdrFile)
239:     {
240:       root = new ArkDirectory(null, ROOT_DIR);
241:       contentFileMeta = hdrFile.GetStream();
242:       var header = contentFileMeta;
243:       header.Position = 8;
244:       long fileTableOffset = header.ReadUInt32LE();
245:       uint numFiles = header.ReadUInt32LE();
246:       long dirTableOffset = header.ReadUInt32LE();
247:       string[] dirs = new string[header.ReadUInt32LE()];
248:       header.Position = 0x24;
249:       long blockSize = header.ReadUInt32LE();
250:       header.Position = dirTableOffset;
251:       for(int dir = 0; dir < dirs.Length; dir++)
252:       {
253:         header.Position = dirTableOffset + (8 * dir) + 4;
254:         header.Position = header.ReadUInt32LE();
255:         dirs[dir] = header.ReadASCIINullTerminated();
256:       }
257:       for(int file = 0; file < numFiles; file++)
258:       {
259:         header.Position = fileTableOffset + (24 * file) + 4;
260:         long filenameOffset = header.ReadUInt32LE();
261:         int dir = header.ReadUInt16LE();
262:         uint blockOffset = header.ReadUInt16LE();
263:         uint block = header.ReadUInt32LE();
264:         uint compressedSize = header.ReadUInt32LE();
265:         header.Position = filenameOffset;
266:         string filename = header.ReadASCIINullTerminated();
267:         ArkDirectory parent = dir > 0 ? makeOrGetDir(dirs[dir]) : root;
268:         parent.AddFile(new OffsetFile(filename, parent, contentFileMeta, block * blockSize + blockOffset,
269:           compressedSize));
270:       }
271:     }
272: 
273:     /// <summary>
274:     /// Read the filename table, which is a blob of strings,
275:     /// then read the filename pointer table which links files to filenames
276:     /// </summary>
277:     private void readFileTable(Stream header, uint version, bool brokenv4)
278:     {
279:       string[] fileNames = readFileNames(header, version != 1);
280:       if (version > 2)
281:       {
282:         // Version 3+:
283:         // Go to end of the filename pointer table which we already read
284:         //               filename blob               filename pointer table
285:         header.Seek(fileNameTableOffset + fileNameTableSize + 4 + 4 * numFileNames, SeekOrigin.Begin);
286:       }
287:       else
288:       {
289:         // Version 2: still at beginning of file. (after version number ofc)
290:         header.Seek(4, SeekOrigin.Begin);
291:       }
292:       // Now the number of *actual* files in the archive.
293:       // Directories are not explicitly stored. Rather, they are inferred
294:       // by the path string each file has, which tells you in which folder
295:       // the file lives.
296:       uint numFiles = header.ReadUInt32LE();
297:       for (var i = 0; i < numFiles; i++)
298:       {
299:         // Version 3 uses 32-bit file offsets
300:         long arkFileOffset = 0;
301:         if (version != 1) arkFileOffset = (brokenv4 || version <= 3 ? header.ReadUInt32LE() : header.ReadInt64LE());
302:         int filenameStringId = header.ReadInt32LE();
303:         int dirStringId = header.ReadInt32LE();
304:         if (version == 1) arkFileOffset = header.ReadUInt32LE();
305:         uint size = header.ReadUInt32LE();
306:         uint zero = header.ReadUInt32LE();
307:         // Version 7 uses this differently. now, files marked as 0 should be skipped,
308:         // while NON-zero values mean real files. I think.
309:         if ((version == 7 && zero != 0) || (version != 7 && zero == 0))
310:         {
311:           ArkDirectory parent = dirStringId > 0 ? makeOrGetDir(fileNames[dirStringId]) : root;
312:           parent.AddFile(new OffsetFile(fileNames[filenameStringId], parent, contentFileMeta, arkFileOffset, size));
313:         }
314:       }
315:     }
316: 
317:     private string[] readFileNames(Stream header, bool nullTerminated)
318:     {
319:       fileNameTableSize = header.ReadUInt32LE();
320: 
321:       if (!nullTerminated)
322:       {
323:         // Reads array of fixed-length strings
324:         string[] strings = new string[fileNameTableSize];
325:         for (int i = 0; i < fileNameTableSize; i++)
326:           strings[i] = header.ReadLengthUTF8();
327: 
328:         return strings;
329:       }
330: 
331:       // Save position of filename table for later.
332:       fileNameTableOffset = header.Position;
333:       // Skip past filename table, since we don't yet know where all the strings are
334:       header.Seek(fileNameTableSize, SeekOrigin.Current);
335: 
336:       // Rather than read all filenames with their offsets, we read all the
337:       // offsets first, then read the filenames. This saves a lot of seeking
338:       // back-and-forth within the header.
339:       numFileNames = header.ReadUInt32LE();
340:       if (numFileNames > fileNameTableSize)
341:       {
342:         throw new InvalidDataException("Ark header appears to be invalid (number of filenames exceeds filename table size).");
343:       }
344:       long[] fileNameOffsets = new long[numFileNames];
345:       for (var i = 0; i < numFileNames; i++)
346:       {
347:         fileNameOffsets[i] = header.ReadInt32LE();
348:       }
349:       string[] fileNames = new string[numFileNames];
350:       for (var i = 0; i < numFileNames; i++)
351:       {
352:         if (fileNameOffsets[i] != 0)
353:         {
354:           header.Seek(fileNameTableOffset + fileNameOffsets[i], SeekOrigin.Begin);
355:           fileNames[i] = header.ReadASCIINullTerminated();
356:         }
357:         else
358:           fileNames[i] = null;
359:       }
360:       return fileNames;
361:     }
362: 
363:     /// <summary>
364:     /// Reads the new file table format in v9 and v10
365:     /// </summary>
366:     private void readNewFileTable(Stream header, bool readHash = false)
367:     {
368:       uint numFiles = header.ReadUInt32LE();
369:       var files = new OffsetFile[numFiles];
370: 
371:       for (var i = 0; i < numFiles; i++)
372:       {
373:         // Version 3 uses 32-bit file offsets
374:         long arkFileOffset = header.ReadInt64LE();
375:         string path = header.ReadLengthPrefixedString(System.Text.Encoding.UTF8);
376:         var flags = header.ReadInt32LE();
377:         uint size = header.ReadUInt32LE();
378:         if (readHash) header.Seek(4, SeekOrigin.Current); // Skips checksum
379: 
380:         var finalSlash = path.LastIndexOf('/');
381:         var fileDir = path.Substring(0, finalSlash < 0 ? 0 : finalSlash);
382:         var fileName = path.Substring(finalSlash < 0 ? 0 : (finalSlash + 1));
383:         var parent = makeOrGetDir(fileDir);
384:         var file = new OffsetFile(fileName, parent, contentFileMeta, arkFileOffset, size);
385:         file.ExtendedInfo["id"] = i;
386:         file.ExtendedInfo["flags"] = flags;
387:         files[i] = file;
388:         parent.AddFile(file);
389:       }
390: 
391:       var numFiles2 = header.ReadUInt32LE();
392:       if(numFiles != numFiles2)
393:         throw new Exception("Ark header appears invalid (file count mismatch)");
394:       for(var i = 0; i < numFiles2; i++)
395:       {
396:         files[i].ExtendedInfo["flags2"] = header.ReadInt32LE();
397:       }
398: 
399: 
400:     }
401: 
402:     /// <summary>
403:     /// Get the directory at the end of this path, or make it (and all
404:     /// intermediate dirs) if it doesn't exist.
405:     /// </summary>
406:     /// <param name="path"></param>
407:     /// <returns></returns>
408:     private ArkDirectory makeOrGetDir(string path)
409:     {
410:       if(path == null || path == "")
411:       {
412:         path = ".";
413:       }
414:       string[] breadcrumbs = path.Split('/');
415:       IDirectory last = root;
416:       IDirectory current;
417:       if(breadcrumbs[0] == "." && breadcrumbs.Length == 1)
418:       {
419:         return root;
420:       }
421: 
422:       for (var idx = 0; idx < breadcrumbs.Length; idx++)
423:       {
424:         if (!last.TryGetDirectory(breadcrumbs[idx], out current))
425:         {
426:           current = new ArkDirectory(last, breadcrumbs[idx]);
427:           (last as ArkDirectory).AddDir(current as ArkDirectory);
428:         }
429:         last = current;
430:       }
431:       return last as ArkDirectory;
432:     }
433: 
434:     #region IDisposable Support
435:     private bool disposedValue = false; // To detect redundant calls
436: 
437:     protected virtual void Dispose(bool disposing)
438:     {
439:       if (!disposedValue)
440:       {
441:         if (disposing)
442:         {
443:           // TODO: dispose managed state (managed objects).
444:         }
445:         contentFileMeta.Close();
446:         contentFileMeta.Dispose();
447:         // TODO: free unmanaged resources (unmanaged objects) and override a finalizer below.
448:         // TODO: set large fields to null.
449: 
450:         disposedValue = true;
451:       }
452:     }
453: 
454:     // TODO: override a finalizer only if Dispose(bool disposing) above has code to free unmanaged resources.
455:     // ~ArkPackage() {
456:     //   // Do not change this code. Put cleanup code in Dispose(bool disposing) above.
457:     //   Dispose(false);
458:     // }
459: 
460:     // This code added to correctly implement the disposable pattern.
461:     public override void Dispose()
462:     {
463:       // Do not change this code. Put cleanup code in Dispose(bool disposing) above.
464:       Dispose(true);
465:       // TODO: uncomment the following line if the finalizer is overridden above.
466:       // GC.SuppressFinalize(this);
467:     }
468:     #endregion
469:   }
470: }

(End of file - total 470 lines)
```

## Assistant (Build · gemma-4-31b-it · 45.4s)

_Thinking:_

`PkgTool.Core` doesn't seem to support `.ark` files.

I'll try to use a simple Python script to extract the files from the `.ark` archives.

The `ArkPackage.cs` shows that the files are `OffsetFile`s. This usually means there's a table of offsets and sizes.

Let's try to write a Python script that parses the `.ark` header and extracts the files.

I'll use the logic from `ArkPackage.cs`.

Version 10 is the highest version.

Let's try to implement a basic `ArkExtractor` in Python.

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "import os\nimport struct\n\ndef read_uint32_le(f):\n    return struct.unpack('<I', f.read(4))[0]\n\ndef read_int32_le(f):\n    return struct.unpack('<i', f.read(4))[0]\n\ndef read_int64_le(f):\n    return struct.unpack('<q', f.read(8))[0]\n\ndef read_length_utf8(f):\n    length = read_uint32_le(f)\n    return f.read(length).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')\n\ndef read_ascii_null_terminated(f):\n    res = b\"\"\n    while True:\n        char = f.read(1)\n        if not char or char == b\"\\\\x00\":\n            break\n        res += char\n    return res.decode('ascii', errors='replace')\n\ndef extract_ark(ark_path, output_dir):\n    with open(ark_path, 'rb') as f:\n        version = read_uint32_le(f)\n        \n        if version == 0x4B5241: # \"ARK\"\n            # Old ark format\n            f.seek(8)\n            file_table_offset = read_uint32_le(f)\n            num_files = read_uint32_le(f)\n            dir_table_offset = read_uint32_le(f)\n            num_dirs = read_uint32_le(f)\n            \n            # Read files\n            for i in range(num_files):\n                f.seek(file_table_offset + (24 * i) + 4)\n                filename_offset = read_uint32_le(f)\n                dir_id = struct.unpack('<H', f.read(2))[0]\n                block_offset = struct.unpack('<H', f.read(2))[0]\n                block = read_uint32_le(f)\n                size = read_uint32_le(f)\n                \n                f.seek(filename_offset)\n                filename = read_ascii_null_terminated(f)\n                \n                parent_dir = dirs[dir_id] if dir_id < len(dirs) else \"\"\n                out_path = os.path.join(output_dir, parent_dir, filename)\n                os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(out_path), exist_ok=True)\n                \n                # We can ignore the paths for now and just use the current file\n                    f.seek(num_paths * 0, 1) # This is wrong, we need to read the strings\n                    # Actually, let's just read them to skip\n                    for i in range(num_paths):\n                        read_length_utf8(f)\n                    \n                    if 6 <= version <= 9:\n                        num_checksums = read_uint32_le(f)\n                        f.seek(4 * num_checksums, 1)\n                else:\n                    # ## Assistant (Build · gemma-4-31b-it · 32.5s)
```

_Thinking:_

It failed. I probably have the version or the reading logic wrong.

Let's look at the `.ark` header again.
`00000000  01 01 00 00 00 05 00 01  00 21 00 00 00 0a 00 00`
The first 4 bytes are `01 01 00 00`. That's `1` in little endian. So version = 1.

In my script:
`if 1 <= version <= 10:`
And then it goes to:
`if version > 2: ...`
But version is 1, so it goes to:
`if version < 8: ...`
But I left that block empty!

I need to implement the `readFileTable` for version 1.

**Tool: edit**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "oldString": "            if version < 8:\n                # read old file table (Version 1, 2)\n                # This is complex because it involves reading filename strings first\n                # Let's skip for now and try a simpler approach if possible\n                pass",
  "newString": "            if version < 8:\n                # read old file table (Version 1, 2)\n                # Version 1,2: file records are read.\n                # According to ArkPackage.cs:\n                # numRecords = header.ReadUInt32LE();\n                # header.Close();\n                # contentFileMeta = hdrFile.GetStream();\n                # contentFileMeta.Seek(8 + numRecords * 20, SeekOrigin.Begin);\n                # readFileTable(contentFileMeta, version, brokenv4);\n                \n                num_records = read_uint32_le(f)\n                # In version 1, we skip to the file table\n                # Actually, let's try to find where the files are.\n                # The C# code says: contentFileMeta.Seek(8 + numRecords * 20, SeekOrigin.Begin);\n                # Then it calls readFileTable.\n                # In readFileTable:\n                # string[] fileNames = readFileNames(header, version != 1);\n                # For version 1, nullTerminated = false.\n                # readFileNames (nullTerminated=false):\n                # fileNameTableSize = header.ReadUInt32LE();\n                # string[] strings = new string[fileNameTableSize];\n                # for (int i = 0; i < fileNameTableSize; i++)\n                #   strings[i] = header.ReadLengthUTF8();\n                \n                f.seek(8 + num_records * 20)\n                \n                # read filenames\n                filename_table_size = read_uint32_le(f)\n                filenames = []\n                for i in range(filename_table_size):\n                    filenames.append(read_length_utf8(f))\n                \n                # Now the actual files\n                num_files = read_uint32_le(f)\n                for i in range(num_files):\n                    # Version 1: offset is read at the end\n                    # For version != 1, it's read first.\n                    #- Read filename pointer\n                    #- Read dir pointer\n                    #- Read block offset\n                    #- Read block\n                    #- Read size\n                    #- Read zero\n                    # - Read offset (for version 1)\n                    \n                    # Let's try to mimic the C# loop\n                    # if (version != 1) arkFileOffset = ...\n                    # filenameStringId = readInt32LE();\n                    # dirStringId = readInt32LE();\n                    # if (version == 1) arkFileOffset = readUInt32LE();\n                    # size = readUInt32LE();\n                    # zero = readUInt32LE();\n                    \n                    filename_id = read_int32_le(f)\n                    dir_id = read_int32_le(f)\n                    ark_offset = read_uint32_le(f)\n                    size = read_uint32_le(f)\n                    zero = read_uint32_le(f)\n                    \n                    filename = filenames[filename_id] if filename_id < len(filenames) else \"unknown\"\n                    parent_dir = filenames[dir_id] if dir_id < len(filenames) else \"\"\n                    \n                    out_path = os.path.join(output_dir, parent_dir, filename)\n                    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(out_path), exist_ok=True)\n                    \n                    f.seek(ark_offset)\n                    with open(out_path, 'wb') as out:\n                        out.write(f.read(size))\n",
```
